FOR ALL YOU DRUNKS IN A DRY COUNTY
SUGAR WINE:
IN AN EMPTY MILK JUG PUT 2 CUPS SUGAR. 1 CUP WELCH'S GRAPE JUICE FROM CONCENTRATE (MUST BE WELCHS). 1/2 TSP OF YEAST.
FILL WITH LUKEWARM WATER UPTO 3 INCHES FROM THE TOP. POKE HOLES IN BALLOON WITH A PIN. PLACE BALLOON OVER THE TOP.
WAIT 21 DAYS. THEN FLAVOR WITH FAVORITE KOOLAID
